    "              'max': rankingsreduced.max(),\n",
    "              'median': rankingsreduced.median(),\n",
    "              'length': len(rankingsreduced),\n",
    "              'miss.val': rankingsreduced.isnull().sum(),\n",
    "             })"
   ]

   "source": [
    "# the indexes of 1 tell us that the car is Petrol and 0 tell us that it is not, same for Diesel"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "id": "8dfb88d3",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "# The general rule is to use one fewer dummy variables than categories. So for quarterly data, use three dummy variables; for monthly data, use 11 dummy variables; and for daily data, use six dummy variables, and so on. Howeevr for this large data set we only need one less dummy variable than the number of categories."
   ]
  },
  {
